9 /// \file This pass tries to apply several peephole SDWA patterns. ----
10 /// ----
11 /// E.g. original: ----
12 /// V_LSHRREV_B32_e32 %0, 16, %1 ----
13 /// V_ADD_CO_U32_e32 %2, %0, %3 ----
14 /// V_LSHLREV_B32_e32 %4, 16, %2 ----
15 /// ----
16 /// Replace: ----
17 /// V_ADD_CO_U32_sdwa %4, %1, %3 ----
18 /// dst_sel:WORD_1 dst_unused:UNUSED_PAD src0_sel:WORD_1 src1_sel:DWORD ----
19 /// ----
20 //===----------------------------------------------------------------------===// ----
21 ----

246 static void copyRegOperand(MachineOperand &To, const MachineOperand &From) { 0
247 assert(To.isReg() && From.isReg()); 0
248 To.setReg(From.getReg()); 0
249 To.setSubReg(From.getSubReg()); 0
250 To.setIsUndef(From.isUndef()); 0
251 if (To.isUse()) { 0
252 To.setIsKill(From.isKill()); 0
253 } else { ----
254 To.setIsDead(From.isDead()); 0
255 } ----
256 } 0

258 static bool isSameReg(const MachineOperand &LHS, const MachineOperand &RHS) { 0
259 return LHS.isReg() && 0
260 RHS.isReg() && 0
261 LHS.getReg() == RHS.getReg() && 0
262 LHS.getSubReg() == RHS.getSubReg(); 0
263 } ----
264 ----
265 static MachineOperand *findSingleRegUse(const MachineOperand *Reg, 0
266 const MachineRegisterInfo *MRI) { ----
267 if (!Reg->isReg() || !Reg->isDef()) 0
268 return nullptr; 0
269 ----
270 MachineOperand *ResMO = nullptr; 0
271 for (MachineOperand &UseMO : MRI->use_nodbg_operands(Reg->getReg())) { 0
272 // If there exist use of subreg of Reg then return nullptr ----
273 if (!isSameReg(UseMO, *Reg)) 0
274 return nullptr; 0
275 ----
276 // Check that there is only one instruction that uses Reg ----
277 if (!ResMO) { 0
278 ResMO = &UseMO; 0
279 } else if (ResMO->getParent() != UseMO.getParent()) { 0
280 return nullptr; 0
281 } ----
282 } ----
283 ----
284 return ResMO; 0
285 } ----
286 ----
287 static MachineOperand *findSingleRegDef(const MachineOperand *Reg, 0
288 const MachineRegisterInfo *MRI) { ----
289 if (!Reg->isReg()) 0
290 return nullptr; 0
291 ----
292 MachineInstr *DefInstr = MRI->getUniqueVRegDef(Reg->getReg()); 0
293 if (!DefInstr) 0
294 return nullptr; 0
295 ----
296 for (auto &DefMO : DefInstr->defs()) { 0
297 if (DefMO.isReg() && DefMO.getReg() == Reg->getReg()) 0
298 return &DefMO; 0
299 } ----
300 ----
301 // Ignore implicit defs. ----
302 return nullptr; 0
303 } ----

305 uint64_t SDWASrcOperand::getSrcMods(const SIInstrInfo *TII, 0
306 const MachineOperand *SrcOp) const { ----
307 uint64_t Mods = 0; 0
308 const auto *MI = SrcOp->getParent(); 0
309 if (TII->getNamedOperand(*MI, AMDGPU::OpName::src0) == SrcOp) { 0
310 if (auto *Mod = TII->getNamedOperand(*MI, AMDGPU::OpName::src0_modifiers)) { 0
311 Mods = Mod->getImm(); 0
312 } ----
313 } else if (TII->getNamedOperand(*MI, AMDGPU::OpName::src1) == SrcOp) { 0
314 if (auto *Mod = TII->getNamedOperand(*MI, AMDGPU::OpName::src1_modifiers)) { 0
315 Mods = Mod->getImm(); 0
316 } ----
317 } ----
318 if (Abs || Neg) { 0
319 assert(!Sext && 0
320 "Float and integer src modifiers can't be set simultaneously"); ----
321 Mods |= Abs ? SISrcMods::ABS : 0u; 0
322 Mods ^= Neg ? SISrcMods::NEG : 0u; 0
323 } else if (Sext) { 0
324 Mods |= SISrcMods::SEXT; 0
325 } ----
326 ----
327 return Mods; 0
328 } ----

330 MachineInstr *SDWASrcOperand::potentialToConvert(const SIInstrInfo *TII) { 0
331 // For SDWA src operand potential instruction is one that use register ----
332 // defined by parent instruction ----
333 MachineOperand *PotentialMO = findSingleRegUse(getReplacedOperand(), getMRI()); 0
334 if (!PotentialMO) 0
335 return nullptr; 0
336 ----
337 return PotentialMO->getParent(); 0
338 } ----

340 bool SDWASrcOperand::convertToSDWA(MachineInstr &MI, const SIInstrInfo *TII) { 0
341 // Find operand in instruction that matches source operand and replace it with ----
342 // target operand. Set corresponding src_sel ----
343 bool IsPreserveSrc = false; 0
344 MachineOperand *Src = TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::src0); 0
345 MachineOperand *SrcSel = TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::src0_sel); 0
346 MachineOperand *SrcMods = ----
347 TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::src0_modifiers); 0
348 assert(Src && (Src->isReg() || Src->isImm())); 0
349 if (!isSameReg(*Src, *getReplacedOperand())) { 0
350 // If this is not src0 then it could be src1 ----
351 Src = TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::src1); 0
352 SrcSel = TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::src1_sel); 0
353 SrcMods = TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::src1_modifiers); 0
354 ----
355 if (!Src || 0
356 !isSameReg(*Src, *getReplacedOperand())) { 0
357 // It's possible this Src is a tied operand for ----
358 // UNUSED_PRESERVE, in which case we can either ----
359 // abandon the peephole attempt, or if legal we can ----
360 // copy the target operand into the tied slot ----
361 // if the preserve operation will effectively cause the same ----
362 // result by overwriting the rest of the dst. ----
363 MachineOperand *Dst = TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::vdst); 0
364 MachineOperand *DstUnused = ----
365 TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::dst_unused); 0
366 ----
367 if (Dst && 0
368 DstUnused->getImm() == AMDGPU::SDWA::DstUnused::UNUSED_PRESERVE) { 0
369 // This will work if the tied src is accessing WORD_0, and the dst is ----
370 // writing WORD_1. Modifiers don't matter because all the bits that ----
371 // would be impacted are being overwritten by the dst. ----
372 // Any other case will not work. ----
373 SdwaSel DstSel = static_cast( ----
374 TII->getNamedImmOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::dst_sel)); 0
375 if (DstSel == AMDGPU::SDWA::SdwaSel::WORD_1 && 0
376 getSrcSel() == AMDGPU::SDWA::SdwaSel::WORD_0) { 0
377 IsPreserveSrc = true; 0
378 auto DstIdx = AMDGPU::getNamedOperandIdx(MI.getOpcode(), 0
379 AMDGPU::OpName::vdst); ----
380 auto TiedIdx = MI.findTiedOperandIdx(DstIdx); 0
381 Src = &MI.getOperand(TiedIdx); 0
382 SrcSel = nullptr; 0
383 SrcMods = nullptr; 0
384 } else { ----
385 // Not legal to convert this src ----
386 return false; 0
387 } ----
388 } ----
389 } ----
390 assert(Src && Src->isReg()); 0
391 ----
392 if ((MI.getOpcode() == AMDGPU::V_FMAC_F16_sdwa || 0
393 MI.getOpcode() == AMDGPU::V_FMAC_F32_sdwa || 0
394 MI.getOpcode() == AMDGPU::V_MAC_F16_sdwa || 0
395 MI.getOpcode() == AMDGPU::V_MAC_F32_sdwa) && 0
396 !isSameReg(*Src, *getReplacedOperand())) { 0
397 // In case of v_mac_f16/32_sdwa this pass can try to apply src operand to ----
398 // src2. This is not allowed. ----
399 return false; 0
400 } ----
401 ----
402 assert(isSameReg(*Src, *getReplacedOperand()) && 0
403 (IsPreserveSrc || (SrcSel && SrcMods))); ----
404 } ----
405 copyRegOperand(*Src, *getTargetOperand()); 0
406 if (!IsPreserveSrc) { 0
407 SrcSel->setImm(getSrcSel()); 0
408 SrcMods->setImm(getSrcMods(TII, Src)); 0
409 } ----
410 getTargetOperand()->setIsKill(false); 0
411 return true; 0
412 } ----

414 MachineInstr *SDWADstOperand::potentialToConvert(const SIInstrInfo *TII) { 0
415 // For SDWA dst operand potential instruction is one that defines register ----
416 // that this operand uses ----
417 MachineRegisterInfo *MRI = getMRI(); 0
418 MachineInstr *ParentMI = getParentInst(); 0
419 ----
420 MachineOperand *PotentialMO = findSingleRegDef(getReplacedOperand(), MRI); 0
421 if (!PotentialMO) 0
422 return nullptr; 0
423 ----
424 // Check that ParentMI is the only instruction that uses replaced register ----
425 for (MachineInstr &UseInst : MRI->use_nodbg_instructions(PotentialMO->getReg())) { 0
426 if (&UseInst != ParentMI) 0
427 return nullptr; 0
428 } ----
429 ----
430 return PotentialMO->getParent(); 0
431 } ----
432 ----
433 bool SDWADstOperand::convertToSDWA(MachineInstr &MI, const SIInstrInfo *TII) { 0
434 // Replace vdst operand in MI with target operand. Set dst_sel and dst_unused ----
435 ----
436 if ((MI.getOpcode() == AMDGPU::V_FMAC_F16_sdwa || 0
437 MI.getOpcode() == AMDGPU::V_FMAC_F32_sdwa || 0
438 MI.getOpcode() == AMDGPU::V_MAC_F16_sdwa || 0
439 MI.getOpcode() == AMDGPU::V_MAC_F32_sdwa) && 0
440 getDstSel() != AMDGPU::SDWA::DWORD) { 0
441 // v_mac_f16/32_sdwa allow dst_sel to be equal only to DWORD ----
442 return false; 0
443 } ----
444 ----
445 MachineOperand *Operand = TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::vdst); 0
446 assert(Operand && 0
447 Operand->isReg() && ----
448 isSameReg(*Operand, *getReplacedOperand())); ----
449 copyRegOperand(*Operand, *getTargetOperand()); 0
450 MachineOperand *DstSel= TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::dst_sel); 0
451 assert(DstSel); 0
452 DstSel->setImm(getDstSel()); 0
453 MachineOperand *DstUnused= TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::dst_unused); 0
454 assert(DstUnused); 0
455 DstUnused->setImm(getDstUnused()); 0
456 ----
457 // Remove original instruction because it would conflict with our new ----
458 // instruction by register definition ----
459 getParentInst()->eraseFromParent(); 0
460 return true; 0
461 } ----
462 ----
463 bool SDWADstPreserveOperand::convertToSDWA(MachineInstr &MI, 0
464 const SIInstrInfo *TII) { ----
465 // MI should be moved right before v_or_b32. ----
466 // For this we should clear all kill flags on uses of MI src-operands or else ----
467 // we can encounter problem with use of killed operand. ----
468 for (MachineOperand &MO : MI.uses()) { 0
469 if (!MO.isReg()) 0
470 continue; 0
471 getMRI()->clearKillFlags(MO.getReg()); 0
472 } ----
473 ----
474 // Move MI before v_or_b32 ----
475 auto MBB = MI.getParent(); 0
476 MBB->remove(&MI); 0
477 MBB->insert(getParentInst(), &MI); 0
478 ----
479 // Add Implicit use of preserved register ----
480 MachineInstrBuilder MIB(*MBB->getParent(), MI); 0
481 MIB.addReg(getPreservedOperand()->getReg(), 0
482 RegState::ImplicitKill, ----
483 getPreservedOperand()->getSubReg()); ----
484 ----
485 // Tie dst to implicit use ----
486 MI.tieOperands(AMDGPU::getNamedOperandIdx(MI.getOpcode(), AMDGPU::OpName::vdst), 0
487 MI.getNumOperands() - 1); 0
488 ----
489 // Convert MI as any other SDWADstOperand and remove v_or_b32 ----
490 return SDWADstOperand::convertToSDWA(MI, TII); 0
491 } ----
492 ----
493 std::optional ----
494 SIPeepholeSDWA::foldToImm(const MachineOperand &Op) const { 0
495 if (Op.isImm()) { 0
496 return Op.getImm(); 0
497 } ----
498 ----
499 // If this is not immediate then it can be copy of immediate value, e.g.: ----
500 // %1 = S_MOV_B32 255; ----
501 if (Op.isReg()) { 0
502 for (const MachineOperand &Def : MRI->def_operands(Op.getReg())) { 0
503 if (!isSameReg(Op, Def)) 0
504 continue; 0
505 ----
506 const MachineInstr *DefInst = Def.getParent(); 0
507 if (!TII->isFoldableCopy(*DefInst)) 0
508 return std::nullopt; 0
509 ----
510 const MachineOperand &Copied = DefInst->getOperand(1); 0
511 if (!Copied.isImm()) 0
512 return std::nullopt; 0
513 ----
514 return Copied.getImm(); 0
515 } ----
516 } ----
517 ----
518 return std::nullopt; 0
519 } ----
520 ----
521 std::unique_ptr ----
522 SIPeepholeSDWA::matchSDWAOperand(MachineInstr &MI) { 0
523 unsigned Opcode = MI.getOpcode(); 0
524 switch (Opcode) { 0
525 case AMDGPU::V_LSHRREV_B32_e32: 0
526 case AMDGPU::V_ASHRREV_I32_e32: ----
527 case AMDGPU::V_LSHLREV_B32_e32: ----
528 case AMDGPU::V_LSHRREV_B32_e64: ----
529 case AMDGPU::V_ASHRREV_I32_e64: ----
530 case AMDGPU::V_LSHLREV_B32_e64: { ----
531 // from: v_lshrrev_b32_e32 v1, 16/24, v0 ----
532 // to SDWA src:v0 src_sel:WORD_1/BYTE_3 ----
533 ----
534 // from: v_ashrrev_i32_e32 v1, 16/24, v0 ----
535 // to SDWA src:v0 src_sel:WORD_1/BYTE_3 sext:1 ----
536 ----
537 // from: v_lshlrev_b32_e32 v1, 16/24, v0 ----
538 // to SDWA dst:v1 dst_sel:WORD_1/BYTE_3 dst_unused:UNUSED_PAD ----
539 MachineOperand *Src0 = TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::src0); 0
540 auto Imm = foldToImm(*Src0); 0
541 if (!Imm) 0
542 break; 0
543 ----
544 if (*Imm != 16 && *Imm != 24) 0
545 break; 0
546 ----
547 MachineOperand *Src1 = TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::src1); 0
548 MachineOperand *Dst = TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::vdst); 0
549 if (Src1->getReg().isPhysical() || Dst->getReg().isPhysical()) 0
550 break; 0
551 ----
552 if (Opcode == AMDGPU::V_LSHLREV_B32_e32 || 0
553 Opcode == AMDGPU::V_LSHLREV_B32_e64) { ----
554 return std::make_unique( 0
555 Dst, Src1, *Imm == 16 ? WORD_1 : BYTE_3, UNUSED_PAD); 0
556 } else { ----
557 return std::make_unique( 0
558 Src1, Dst, *Imm == 16 ? WORD_1 : BYTE_3, false, false, 0
559 Opcode != AMDGPU::V_LSHRREV_B32_e32 && 0
560 Opcode != AMDGPU::V_LSHRREV_B32_e64); 0
561 } ----
562 break; ----
563 } ----
564 ----
565 case AMDGPU::V_LSHRREV_B16_e32: 0
566 case AMDGPU::V_ASHRREV_I16_e32: ----
567 case AMDGPU::V_LSHLREV_B16_e32: ----
568 case AMDGPU::V_LSHRREV_B16_e64: ----
569 case AMDGPU::V_ASHRREV_I16_e64: ----
570 case AMDGPU::V_LSHLREV_B16_e64: { ----
571 // from: v_lshrrev_b16_e32 v1, 8, v0 ----
572 // to SDWA src:v0 src_sel:BYTE_1 ----
573 ----
574 // from: v_ashrrev_i16_e32 v1, 8, v0 ----
575 // to SDWA src:v0 src_sel:BYTE_1 sext:1 ----
576 ----
577 // from: v_lshlrev_b16_e32 v1, 8, v0 ----
578 // to SDWA dst:v1 dst_sel:BYTE_1 dst_unused:UNUSED_PAD ----
579 MachineOperand *Src0 = TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::src0); 0
580 auto Imm = foldToImm(*Src0); 0
581 if (!Imm || *Imm != 8) 0
582 break; 0
583 ----
584 MachineOperand *Src1 = TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::src1); 0
585 MachineOperand *Dst = TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::vdst); 0
586 ----
587 if (Src1->getReg().isPhysical() || Dst->getReg().isPhysical()) 0
588 break; 0
589 ----
590 if (Opcode == AMDGPU::V_LSHLREV_B16_e32 || 0
591 Opcode == AMDGPU::V_LSHLREV_B16_e64) { ----
592 return std::make_unique(Dst, Src1, BYTE_1, UNUSED_PAD); 0
593 } else { ----
594 return std::make_unique( 0
595 Src1, Dst, BYTE_1, false, false, 0
596 Opcode != AMDGPU::V_LSHRREV_B16_e32 && 0
597 Opcode != AMDGPU::V_LSHRREV_B16_e64); 0
598 } ----
599 break; ----
600 } ----
601 ----
602 case AMDGPU::V_BFE_I32_e64: 0
603 case AMDGPU::V_BFE_U32_e64: { ----
604 // e.g.: ----
605 // from: v_bfe_u32 v1, v0, 8, 8 ----
606 // to SDWA src:v0 src_sel:BYTE_1 ----
607 ----
608 // offset | width | src_sel ----
609 // ------------------------ ----
610 // 0 | 8 | BYTE_0 ----
611 // 0 | 16 | WORD_0 ----
612 // 0 | 32 | DWORD ? ----
613 // 8 | 8 | BYTE_1 ----
614 // 16 | 8 | BYTE_2 ----
615 // 16 | 16 | WORD_1 ----
616 // 24 | 8 | BYTE_3 ----
617 ----
618 MachineOperand *Src1 = TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::src1); 0
619 auto Offset = foldToImm(*Src1); 0
620 if (!Offset) 0
621 break; 0
622 ----
623 MachineOperand *Src2 = TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::src2); 0
624 auto Width = foldToImm(*Src2); 0
625 if (!Width) 0
626 break; 0
627 ----
628 SdwaSel SrcSel = DWORD; 0
629 ----
630 if (*Offset == 0 && *Width == 8) 0
631 SrcSel = BYTE_0; 0
632 else if (*Offset == 0 && *Width == 16) 0
633 SrcSel = WORD_0; 0
634 else if (*Offset == 0 && *Width == 32) 0
635 SrcSel = DWORD; 0
636 else if (*Offset == 8 && *Width == 8) 0
637 SrcSel = BYTE_1; 0
638 else if (*Offset == 16 && *Width == 8) 0
639 SrcSel = BYTE_2; 0
640 else if (*Offset == 16 && *Width == 16) 0
641 SrcSel = WORD_1; 0
642 else if (*Offset == 24 && *Width == 8) 0
643 SrcSel = BYTE_3; 0
644 else ----
645 break; 0
646 ----
647 MachineOperand *Src0 = TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::src0); 0
648 MachineOperand *Dst = TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::vdst); 0
649 ----
650 if (Src0->getReg().isPhysical() || Dst->getReg().isPhysical()) 0
651 break; 0
652 ----
653 return std::make_unique( 0
654 Src0, Dst, SrcSel, false, false, Opcode != AMDGPU::V_BFE_U32_e64); 0
655 } ----
656 ----
657 case AMDGPU::V_AND_B32_e32: 0
658 case AMDGPU::V_AND_B32_e64: { ----
659 // e.g.: ----
660 // from: v_and_b32_e32 v1, 0x0000ffff/0x000000ff, v0 ----
661 // to SDWA src:v0 src_sel:WORD_0/BYTE_0 ----
662 ----
663 MachineOperand *Src0 = TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::src0); 0
664 MachineOperand *Src1 = TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::src1); 0
665 auto ValSrc = Src1; 0
666 auto Imm = foldToImm(*Src0); 0
667 ----
668 if (!Imm) { 0
669 Imm = foldToImm(*Src1); 0
670 ValSrc = Src0; 0
671 } ----
672 ----
673 if (!Imm || (*Imm != 0x0000ffff && *Imm != 0x000000ff)) 0
674 break; 0
675 ----
676 MachineOperand *Dst = TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::vdst); 0
677 ----
678 if (ValSrc->getReg().isPhysical() || Dst->getReg().isPhysical()) 0
679 break; 0
680 ----
681 return std::make_unique( 0
682 ValSrc, Dst, *Imm == 0x0000ffff ? WORD_0 : BYTE_0); 0
683 } ----
684 ----
685 case AMDGPU::V_OR_B32_e32: 0
686 case AMDGPU::V_OR_B32_e64: { ----
687 // Patterns for dst_unused:UNUSED_PRESERVE. ----
688 // e.g., from: ----
689 // v_add_f16_sdwa v0, v1, v2 dst_sel:WORD_1 dst_unused:UNUSED_PAD ----
690 // src1_sel:WORD_1 src2_sel:WORD1 ----
691 // v_add_f16_e32 v3, v1, v2 ----
692 // v_or_b32_e32 v4, v0, v3 ----
693 // to SDWA preserve dst:v4 dst_sel:WORD_1 dst_unused:UNUSED_PRESERVE preserve:v3 ----
694 ----
695 // Check if one of operands of v_or_b32 is SDWA instruction ----
696 using CheckRetType = ----
697 std::optional>; ----
698 auto CheckOROperandsForSDWA = ----
699 [&](const MachineOperand *Op1, const MachineOperand *Op2) -> CheckRetType { 0
700 if (!Op1 || !Op1->isReg() || !Op2 || !Op2->isReg()) 0
701 return CheckRetType(std::nullopt); 0
702 ----
703 MachineOperand *Op1Def = findSingleRegDef(Op1, MRI); 0
704 if (!Op1Def) 0
705 return CheckRetType(std::nullopt); 0
706 ----
707 MachineInstr *Op1Inst = Op1Def->getParent(); 0
708 if (!TII->isSDWA(*Op1Inst)) 0
709 return CheckRetType(std::nullopt); 0
710 ----
711 MachineOperand *Op2Def = findSingleRegDef(Op2, MRI); 0
712 if (!Op2Def) 0
713 return CheckRetType(std::nullopt); 0
714 ----
715 return CheckRetType(std::pair(Op1Def, Op2Def)); 0
716 }; 0
717 ----
718 MachineOperand *OrSDWA = TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::src0); 0
719 MachineOperand *OrOther = TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::src1); 0
720 assert(OrSDWA && OrOther); 0
721 auto Res = CheckOROperandsForSDWA(OrSDWA, OrOther); 0
722 if (!Res) { 0
723 OrSDWA = TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::src1); 0
724 OrOther = TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::src0); 0
725 assert(OrSDWA && OrOther); 0
726 Res = CheckOROperandsForSDWA(OrSDWA, OrOther); 0
727 if (!Res) 0
728 break; 0
729 } ----
730 ----
731 MachineOperand *OrSDWADef = Res->first; 0
732 MachineOperand *OrOtherDef = Res->second; 0
733 assert(OrSDWADef && OrOtherDef); 0
734 ----
735 MachineInstr *SDWAInst = OrSDWADef->getParent(); 0
736 MachineInstr *OtherInst = OrOtherDef->getParent(); 0
737 ----
738 // Check that OtherInstr is actually bitwise compatible with SDWAInst = their ----
739 // destination patterns don't overlap. Compatible instruction can be either ----
740 // regular instruction with compatible bitness or SDWA instruction with ----
741 // correct dst_sel ----
742 // SDWAInst | OtherInst bitness / OtherInst dst_sel ----
743 // ----------------------------------------------------- ----
744 // DWORD | no / no ----
745 // WORD_0 | no / BYTE_2/3, WORD_1 ----
746 // WORD_1 | 8/16-bit instructions / BYTE_0/1, WORD_0 ----
747 // BYTE_0 | no / BYTE_1/2/3, WORD_1 ----
748 // BYTE_1 | 8-bit / BYTE_0/2/3, WORD_1 ----
749 // BYTE_2 | 8/16-bit / BYTE_0/1/3. WORD_0 ----
750 // BYTE_3 | 8/16/24-bit / BYTE_0/1/2, WORD_0 ----
751 // E.g. if SDWAInst is v_add_f16_sdwa dst_sel:WORD_1 then v_add_f16 is OK ----
752 // but v_add_f32 is not. ----
753 ----
754 // TODO: add support for non-SDWA instructions as OtherInst. ----
755 // For now this only works with SDWA instructions. For regular instructions ----
756 // there is no way to determine if the instruction writes only 8/16/24-bit ----
757 // out of full register size and all registers are at min 32-bit wide. ----
758 if (!TII->isSDWA(*OtherInst)) 0
759 break; 0
760 ----
761 SdwaSel DstSel = static_cast( 0
762 TII->getNamedImmOperand(*SDWAInst, AMDGPU::OpName::dst_sel)); 0
763 SdwaSel OtherDstSel = static_cast( ----
764 TII->getNamedImmOperand(*OtherInst, AMDGPU::OpName::dst_sel)); 0
765 ----
766 bool DstSelAgree = false; 0
767 switch (DstSel) { 0
768 case WORD_0: DstSelAgree = ((OtherDstSel == BYTE_2) || 0
769 (OtherDstSel == BYTE_3) || 0
770 (OtherDstSel == WORD_1)); ----
771 break; 0
772 case WORD_1: DstSelAgree = ((OtherDstSel == BYTE_0) || 0
773 (OtherDstSel == BYTE_1) || 0
774 (OtherDstSel == WORD_0)); ----
775 break; 0
776 case BYTE_0: DstSelAgree = ((OtherDstSel == BYTE_1) || 0
777 (OtherDstSel == BYTE_2) || 0
778 (OtherDstSel == BYTE_3) || 0
779 (OtherDstSel == WORD_1)); ----
780 break; 0
781 case BYTE_1: DstSelAgree = ((OtherDstSel == BYTE_0) || 0
782 (OtherDstSel == BYTE_2) || 0
783 (OtherDstSel == BYTE_3) || 0
784 (OtherDstSel == WORD_1)); ----
785 break; 0
786 case BYTE_2: DstSelAgree = ((OtherDstSel == BYTE_0) || 0
787 (OtherDstSel == BYTE_1) || 0
788 (OtherDstSel == BYTE_3) || 0
789 (OtherDstSel == WORD_0)); ----
790 break; 0
791 case BYTE_3: DstSelAgree = ((OtherDstSel == BYTE_0) || 0
792 (OtherDstSel == BYTE_1) || 0
793 (OtherDstSel == BYTE_2) || 0
794 (OtherDstSel == WORD_0)); ----
795 break; 0
796 default: DstSelAgree = false; 0
797 } ----
798 ----
799 if (!DstSelAgree) 0
800 break; 0
801 ----
802 // Also OtherInst dst_unused should be UNUSED_PAD ----
803 DstUnused OtherDstUnused = static_cast( ----
804 TII->getNamedImmOperand(*OtherInst, AMDGPU::OpName::dst_unused)); 0
805 if (OtherDstUnused != DstUnused::UNUSED_PAD) 0
806 break; 0
807 ----
808 // Create DstPreserveOperand ----
809 MachineOperand *OrDst = TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::vdst); 0
810 assert(OrDst && OrDst->isReg()); 0
811 ----
812 return std::make_unique( 0
813 OrDst, OrSDWADef, OrOtherDef, DstSel); 0
814 ----
815 } ----
816 } ----
817 ----
818 return std::unique_ptr(nullptr); 0
819 } ----
820 ----
821 #if !defined(NDEBUG) ----
822 static raw_ostream& operator<<(raw_ostream &OS, const SDWAOperand &Operand) { 0
823 Operand.print(OS); 0
824 return OS; 0
825 } ----
826 #endif ----
827 ----
828 void SIPeepholeSDWA::matchSDWAOperands(MachineBasicBlock &MBB) { 0
829 for (MachineInstr &MI : MBB) { 0
830 if (auto Operand = matchSDWAOperand(MI)) { 0
831 LLVM_DEBUG(dbgs() << "Match: " << MI << "To: " << *Operand << '\n'); 0
832 SDWAOperands[&MI] = std::move(Operand); 0
833 ++NumSDWAPatternsFound; 0
834 } 0
835 } ----
836 } 0
837 ----
838 // Convert the V_ADD_CO_U32_e64 into V_ADD_CO_U32_e32. This allows ----
839 // isConvertibleToSDWA to perform its transformation on V_ADD_CO_U32_e32 into ----
840 // V_ADD_CO_U32_sdwa. ----
841 // ----
842 // We are transforming from a VOP3 into a VOP2 form of the instruction. ----
843 // %19:vgpr_32 = V_AND_B32_e32 255, ----
844 // killed %16:vgpr_32, implicit $exec ----
845 // %47:vgpr_32, %49:sreg_64_xexec = V_ADD_CO_U32_e64 ----
846 // %26.sub0:vreg_64, %19:vgpr_32, implicit $exec ----
847 // %48:vgpr_32, dead %50:sreg_64_xexec = V_ADDC_U32_e64 ----
848 // %26.sub1:vreg_64, %54:vgpr_32, killed %49:sreg_64_xexec, implicit $exec ----
849 // ----
850 // becomes ----
851 // %47:vgpr_32 = V_ADD_CO_U32_sdwa ----
852 // 0, %26.sub0:vreg_64, 0, killed %16:vgpr_32, 0, 6, 0, 6, 0, ----
853 // implicit-def $vcc, implicit $exec ----
854 // %48:vgpr_32, dead %50:sreg_64_xexec = V_ADDC_U32_e64 ----
855 // %26.sub1:vreg_64, %54:vgpr_32, killed $vcc, implicit $exec ----
856 void SIPeepholeSDWA::pseudoOpConvertToVOP2(MachineInstr &MI, 0
857 const GCNSubtarget &ST) const { ----
858 int Opc = MI.getOpcode(); 0
859 assert((Opc == AMDGPU::V_ADD_CO_U32_e64 || Opc == AMDGPU::V_SUB_CO_U32_e64) && 0
860 "Currently only handles V_ADD_CO_U32_e64 or V_SUB_CO_U32_e64"); ----
861 ----
862 // Can the candidate MI be shrunk? ----
863 if (!TII->canShrink(MI, *MRI)) 0
864 return; 0
865 Opc = AMDGPU::getVOPe32(Opc); 0
866 // Find the related ADD instruction. ----
867 const MachineOperand *Sdst = TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::sdst); 0
868 if (!Sdst) 0
869 return; 0
870 MachineOperand *NextOp = findSingleRegUse(Sdst, MRI); 0
871 if (!NextOp) 0
872 return; 0
873 MachineInstr &MISucc = *NextOp->getParent(); 0
874 ----
875 // Make sure the carry in/out are subsequently unused. ----
876 MachineOperand *CarryIn = TII->getNamedOperand(MISucc, AMDGPU::OpName::src2); 0
877 if (!CarryIn) 0
878 return; 0
879 MachineOperand *CarryOut = TII->getNamedOperand(MISucc, AMDGPU::OpName::sdst); 0
880 if (!CarryOut) 0
881 return; 0
882 if (!MRI->hasOneUse(CarryIn->getReg()) || !MRI->use_empty(CarryOut->getReg())) 0
883 return; 0
884 // Make sure VCC or its subregs are dead before MI. ----
885 MachineBasicBlock &MBB = *MI.getParent(); 0
886 auto Liveness = MBB.computeRegisterLiveness(TRI, AMDGPU::VCC, MI, 25); 0
887 if (Liveness != MachineBasicBlock::LQR_Dead) 0
888 return; 0
889 // Check if VCC is referenced in range of (MI,MISucc]. ----
890 for (auto I = std::next(MI.getIterator()), E = MISucc.getIterator(); 0
891 I != E; ++I) { 0
892 if (I->modifiesRegister(AMDGPU::VCC, TRI)) 0
893 return; 0
894 } ----
895 ----
896 // Replace MI with V_{SUB|ADD}_I32_e32 ----
897 BuildMI(MBB, MI, MI.getDebugLoc(), TII->get(Opc)) 0
898 .add(*TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::vdst)) 0
899 .add(*TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::src0)) 0
900 .add(*TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::src1)) 0
901 .setMIFlags(MI.getFlags()); 0
902 ----
903 MI.eraseFromParent(); 0
904 ----
905 // Since the carry output of MI is now VCC, update its use in MISucc. ----
906 ----
907 MISucc.substituteRegister(CarryIn->getReg(), TRI->getVCC(), 0, *TRI); 0
908 } ----
909 ----
910 bool SIPeepholeSDWA::isConvertibleToSDWA(MachineInstr &MI, 0
911 const GCNSubtarget &ST) const { ----
912 // Check if this is already an SDWA instruction ----
913 unsigned Opc = MI.getOpcode(); 0
914 if (TII->isSDWA(Opc)) 0
915 return true; 0
916 ----
917 // Check if this instruction has opcode that supports SDWA ----
918 if (AMDGPU::getSDWAOp(Opc) == -1) 0
919 Opc = AMDGPU::getVOPe32(Opc); 0
920 ----
921 if (AMDGPU::getSDWAOp(Opc) == -1) 0
922 return false; 0
923 ----
924 if (!ST.hasSDWAOmod() && TII->hasModifiersSet(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::omod)) 0
925 return false; 0
926 ----
927 if (TII->isVOPC(Opc)) { 0
928 if (!ST.hasSDWASdst()) { 0
929 const MachineOperand *SDst = TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::sdst); 0
930 if (SDst && (SDst->getReg() != AMDGPU::VCC && 0
931 SDst->getReg() != AMDGPU::VCC_LO)) 0
932 return false; 0
933 } ----
934 ----
935 if (!ST.hasSDWAOutModsVOPC() && 0
936 (TII->hasModifiersSet(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::clamp) || 0
937 TII->hasModifiersSet(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::omod))) 0
938 return false; 0
939 ----
940 } else if (TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::sdst) || 0
941 !TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::vdst)) { 0
942 return false; 0
943 } ----
944 ----
945 if (!ST.hasSDWAMac() && (Opc == AMDGPU::V_FMAC_F16_e32 || 0
946 Opc == AMDGPU::V_FMAC_F32_e32 || 0
947 Opc == AMDGPU::V_MAC_F16_e32 || 0
948 Opc == AMDGPU::V_MAC_F32_e32)) ----
949 return false; 0
950 ----
951 // Check if target supports this SDWA opcode ----
952 if (TII->pseudoToMCOpcode(Opc) == -1) 0
953 return false; 0
954 ----
955 // FIXME: has SDWA but require handling of implicit VCC use ----
956 if (Opc == AMDGPU::V_CNDMASK_B32_e32) 0
957 return false; 0
958 ----
959 if (MachineOperand *Src0 = TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::src0)) { 0
960 if (!Src0->isReg() && !Src0->isImm()) 0
961 return false; 0
962 } ----
963 ----
964 if (MachineOperand *Src1 = TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::src1)) { 0
965 if (!Src1->isReg() && !Src1->isImm()) 0
966 return false; 0
967 } ----
968 ----
969 return true; 0
970 } ----
971 ----
972 bool SIPeepholeSDWA::convertToSDWA(MachineInstr &MI, 0
973 const SDWAOperandsVector &SDWAOperands) { ----
974 ----
975 LLVM_DEBUG(dbgs() << "Convert instruction:" << MI); 0
976 ----
977 // Convert to sdwa ----
978 int SDWAOpcode; ----
979 unsigned Opcode = MI.getOpcode(); 0
980 if (TII->isSDWA(Opcode)) { 0
981 SDWAOpcode = Opcode; 0
982 } else { ----
983 SDWAOpcode = AMDGPU::getSDWAOp(Opcode); 0
984 if (SDWAOpcode == -1) 0
985 SDWAOpcode = AMDGPU::getSDWAOp(AMDGPU::getVOPe32(Opcode)); 0
986 } ----
987 assert(SDWAOpcode != -1); 0
988 ----
989 const MCInstrDesc &SDWADesc = TII->get(SDWAOpcode); 0
990 ----
991 // Create SDWA version of instruction MI and initialize its operands ----
992 MachineInstrBuilder SDWAInst = ----
993 BuildMI(*MI.getParent(), MI, MI.getDebugLoc(), SDWADesc) 0
994 .setMIFlags(MI.getFlags()); 0
995 ----
996 // Copy dst, if it is present in original then should also be present in SDWA ----
997 MachineOperand *Dst = TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::vdst); 0
998 if (Dst) { 0
999 assert(AMDGPU::hasNamedOperand(SDWAOpcode, AMDGPU::OpName::vdst)); 0
1000 SDWAInst.add(*Dst); 0
1001 } else if ((Dst = TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::sdst))) { 0
1002 assert(Dst && AMDGPU::hasNamedOperand(SDWAOpcode, AMDGPU::OpName::sdst)); 0
1003 SDWAInst.add(*Dst); 0
1004 } else { ----
1005 assert(AMDGPU::hasNamedOperand(SDWAOpcode, AMDGPU::OpName::sdst)); 0
1006 SDWAInst.addReg(TRI->getVCC(), RegState::Define); 0
1007 } ----
1008 ----
1009 // Copy src0, initialize src0_modifiers. All sdwa instructions has src0 and ----
1010 // src0_modifiers (except for v_nop_sdwa, but it can't get here) ----
1011 MachineOperand *Src0 = TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::src0); 0
1012 assert(Src0 && AMDGPU::hasNamedOperand(SDWAOpcode, AMDGPU::OpName::src0) && 0
1013 AMDGPU::hasNamedOperand(SDWAOpcode, AMDGPU::OpName::src0_modifiers)); ----
1014 if (auto *Mod = TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::src0_modifiers)) 0
1015 SDWAInst.addImm(Mod->getImm()); 0
1016 else ----
1017 SDWAInst.addImm(0); 0
1018 SDWAInst.add(*Src0); 0
1019 ----
1020 // Copy src1 if present, initialize src1_modifiers. ----
1021 MachineOperand *Src1 = TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::src1); 0
1022 if (Src1) { 0
1023 assert(AMDGPU::hasNamedOperand(SDWAOpcode, AMDGPU::OpName::src1) && 0
1024 AMDGPU::hasNamedOperand(SDWAOpcode, AMDGPU::OpName::src1_modifiers)); ----
1025 if (auto *Mod = TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::src1_modifiers)) 0
1026 SDWAInst.addImm(Mod->getImm()); 0
1027 else ----
1028 SDWAInst.addImm(0); 0
1029 SDWAInst.add(*Src1); 0
1030 } ----
1031 ----
1032 if (SDWAOpcode == AMDGPU::V_FMAC_F16_sdwa || 0
1033 SDWAOpcode == AMDGPU::V_FMAC_F32_sdwa || 0
1034 SDWAOpcode == AMDGPU::V_MAC_F16_sdwa || 0
1035 SDWAOpcode == AMDGPU::V_MAC_F32_sdwa) { ----
1036 // v_mac_f16/32 has additional src2 operand tied to vdst ----
1037 MachineOperand *Src2 = TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::src2); 0
1038 assert(Src2); 0
1039 SDWAInst.add(*Src2); 0
1040 } ----
1041 ----
1042 // Copy clamp if present, initialize otherwise ----
1043 assert(AMDGPU::hasNamedOperand(SDWAOpcode, AMDGPU::OpName::clamp)); 0
1044 MachineOperand *Clamp = TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::clamp); 0
1045 if (Clamp) { 0
1046 SDWAInst.add(*Clamp); 0
1047 } else { ----
1048 SDWAInst.addImm(0); 0
1049 } ----
1050 ----
1051 // Copy omod if present, initialize otherwise if needed ----
1052 if (AMDGPU::hasNamedOperand(SDWAOpcode, AMDGPU::OpName::omod)) { 0
1053 MachineOperand *OMod = TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::omod); 0
1054 if (OMod) { 0
1055 SDWAInst.add(*OMod); 0
1056 } else { ----
1057 SDWAInst.addImm(0); 0
1058 } ----
1059 } ----
1060 ----
1061 // Copy dst_sel if present, initialize otherwise if needed ----
1062 if (AMDGPU::hasNamedOperand(SDWAOpcode, AMDGPU::OpName::dst_sel)) { 0
1063 MachineOperand *DstSel = TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::dst_sel); 0
1064 if (DstSel) { 0
1065 SDWAInst.add(*DstSel); 0
1066 } else { ----
1067 SDWAInst.addImm(AMDGPU::SDWA::SdwaSel::DWORD); 0
1068 } ----
1069 } ----
1070 ----
1071 // Copy dst_unused if present, initialize otherwise if needed ----
1072 if (AMDGPU::hasNamedOperand(SDWAOpcode, AMDGPU::OpName::dst_unused)) { 0
1073 MachineOperand *DstUnused = TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::dst_unused); 0
1074 if (DstUnused) { 0
1075 SDWAInst.add(*DstUnused); 0
1076 } else { ----
1077 SDWAInst.addImm(AMDGPU::SDWA::DstUnused::UNUSED_PAD); 0
1078 } ----
1079 } ----
1080 ----
1081 // Copy src0_sel if present, initialize otherwise ----
1082 assert(AMDGPU::hasNamedOperand(SDWAOpcode, AMDGPU::OpName::src0_sel)); 0
1083 MachineOperand *Src0Sel = TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::src0_sel); 0
1084 if (Src0Sel) { 0
1085 SDWAInst.add(*Src0Sel); 0
1086 } else { ----
1087 SDWAInst.addImm(AMDGPU::SDWA::SdwaSel::DWORD); 0
1088 } ----
1089 ----
1090 // Copy src1_sel if present, initialize otherwise if needed ----
1091 if (Src1) { 0
1092 assert(AMDGPU::hasNamedOperand(SDWAOpcode, AMDGPU::OpName::src1_sel)); 0
1093 MachineOperand *Src1Sel = TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::src1_sel); 0
1094 if (Src1Sel) { 0
1095 SDWAInst.add(*Src1Sel); 0
1096 } else { ----
1097 SDWAInst.addImm(AMDGPU::SDWA::SdwaSel::DWORD); 0
1098 } ----
1099 } ----
1100 ----
1101 // Check for a preserved register that needs to be copied. ----
1102 auto DstUnused = TII->getNamedOperand(MI, AMDGPU::OpName::dst_unused); 0
1103 if (DstUnused && 0
1104 DstUnused->getImm() == AMDGPU::SDWA::DstUnused::UNUSED_PRESERVE) { 0
1105 // We expect, if we are here, that the instruction was already in it's SDWA form, ----
1106 // with a tied operand. ----
1107 assert(Dst && Dst->isTied()); 0
1108 assert(Opcode == static_cast(SDWAOpcode)); 0
1109 // We also expect a vdst, since sdst can't preserve. ----
1110 auto PreserveDstIdx = AMDGPU::getNamedOperandIdx(SDWAOpcode, AMDGPU::OpName::vdst); 0
1111 assert(PreserveDstIdx != -1); 0
1112 ----
1113 auto TiedIdx = MI.findTiedOperandIdx(PreserveDstIdx); 0
1114 auto Tied = MI.getOperand(TiedIdx); 0
1115 ----
1116 SDWAInst.add(Tied); 0
1117 SDWAInst->tieOperands(PreserveDstIdx, SDWAInst->getNumOperands() - 1); 0
1118 } ----
1119 ----
1120 // Apply all sdwa operand patterns. ----
1121 bool Converted = false; 0
1122 for (auto &Operand : SDWAOperands) { 0
1123 LLVM_DEBUG(dbgs() << *SDWAInst << "\nOperand: " << *Operand); 0
1124 // There should be no intersection between SDWA operands and potential MIs ----
1125 // e.g.: ----
1126 // v_and_b32 v0, 0xff, v1 -> src:v1 sel:BYTE_0 ----
1127 // v_and_b32 v2, 0xff, v0 -> src:v0 sel:BYTE_0 ----
1128 // v_add_u32 v3, v4, v2 ----
1129 // ----
1130 // In that example it is possible that we would fold 2nd instruction into ----
1131 // 3rd (v_add_u32_sdwa) and then try to fold 1st instruction into 2nd (that ----
1132 // was already destroyed). So if SDWAOperand is also a potential MI then do ----
1133 // not apply it. ----
1134 if (PotentialMatches.count(Operand->getParentInst()) == 0) 0
1135 Converted |= Operand->convertToSDWA(*SDWAInst, TII); 0
1136 } ----
1137 if (Converted) { 0
1138 ConvertedInstructions.push_back(SDWAInst); 0
1139 } else { ----
1140 SDWAInst->eraseFromParent(); 0
1141 return false; 0
1142 } ----
1143 ----
1144 LLVM_DEBUG(dbgs() << "\nInto:" << *SDWAInst << '\n'); 0
1145 ++NumSDWAInstructionsPeepholed; 0
1146 ----
1147 MI.eraseFromParent(); 0
1148 return true; 0
1149 } ----
1150 ----
1151 // If an instruction was converted to SDWA it should not have immediates or SGPR ----
1152 // operands (allowed one SGPR on GFX9). Copy its scalar operands into VGPRs. ----
1153 void SIPeepholeSDWA::legalizeScalarOperands(MachineInstr &MI, 0
1154 const GCNSubtarget &ST) const { ----
1155 const MCInstrDesc &Desc = TII->get(MI.getOpcode()); 0
1156 unsigned ConstantBusCount = 0; 0
1157 for (MachineOperand &Op : MI.explicit_uses()) { 0
1158 if (!Op.isImm() && !(Op.isReg() && !TRI->isVGPR(*MRI, Op.getReg()))) 0
1159 continue; 0
1160 ----
1161 unsigned I = Op.getOperandNo(); 0
1162 if (Desc.operands()[I].RegClass == -1 || 0
1163 !TRI->isVSSuperClass(TRI->getRegClass(Desc.operands()[I].RegClass))) 0
1164 continue; 0
1165 ----
1166 if (ST.hasSDWAScalar() && ConstantBusCount == 0 && Op.isReg() && 0
1167 TRI->isSGPRReg(*MRI, Op.getReg())) { 0
1168 ++ConstantBusCount; 0
1169 continue; 0
1170 } ----
1171 ----
1172 Register VGPR = MRI->createVirtualRegister(&AMDGPU::VGPR_32RegClass); 0
1173 auto Copy = BuildMI(*MI.getParent(), MI.getIterator(), MI.getDebugLoc(), 0
1174 TII->get(AMDGPU::V_MOV_B32_e32), VGPR); 0
1175 if (Op.isImm()) 0
1176 Copy.addImm(Op.getImm()); 0
1177 else if (Op.isReg()) 0
1178 Copy.addReg(Op.getReg(), Op.isKill() ? RegState::Kill : 0, 0
1179 Op.getSubReg()); ----
1180 Op.ChangeToRegister(VGPR, false); 0
1181 } ----
1182 } 0
1183 ----
1184 bool SIPeepholeSDWA::runOnMachineFunction(MachineFunction &MF) { 0
1185 const GCNSubtarget &ST = MF.getSubtarget(); 0
1186 ----
1187 if (!ST.hasSDWA() || skipFunction(MF.getFunction())) 0
1188 return false; 0
1189 ----
1190 MRI = &MF.getRegInfo(); 0
1191 TRI = ST.getRegisterInfo(); 0
1192 TII = ST.getInstrInfo(); 0
1193 ----
1194 // Find all SDWA operands in MF. ----
1195 bool Ret = false; 0
1196 for (MachineBasicBlock &MBB : MF) { 0
1197 bool Changed = false; 0
1198 do { 0
1199 // Preprocess the ADD/SUB pairs so they could be SDWA'ed. ----
1200 // Look for a possible ADD or SUB that resulted from a previously lowered ----
1201 // V_{ADD|SUB}_U64_PSEUDO. The function pseudoOpConvertToVOP2 ----
1202 // lowers the pair of instructions into e32 form. ----
1203 matchSDWAOperands(MBB); 0
1204 for (const auto &OperandPair : SDWAOperands) { 0
1205 const auto &Operand = OperandPair.second; 0
1206 MachineInstr *PotentialMI = Operand->potentialToConvert(TII); 0
1207 if (PotentialMI && 0
1208 (PotentialMI->getOpcode() == AMDGPU::V_ADD_CO_U32_e64 || 0
1209 PotentialMI->getOpcode() == AMDGPU::V_SUB_CO_U32_e64)) 0
1210 pseudoOpConvertToVOP2(*PotentialMI, ST); 0
1211 } ----
1212 SDWAOperands.clear(); 0
1213 ----
1214 // Generate potential match list. ----
1215 matchSDWAOperands(MBB); 0
1216 ----
1217 for (const auto &OperandPair : SDWAOperands) { 0
1218 const auto &Operand = OperandPair.second; 0
1219 MachineInstr *PotentialMI = Operand->potentialToConvert(TII); 0
1220 if (PotentialMI && isConvertibleToSDWA(*PotentialMI, ST)) { 0
1221 PotentialMatches[PotentialMI].push_back(Operand.get()); 0
1222 } ----
1223 } ----
1224 ----
1225 for (auto &PotentialPair : PotentialMatches) { 0
1226 MachineInstr &PotentialMI = *PotentialPair.first; 0
1227 convertToSDWA(PotentialMI, PotentialPair.second); 0
1228 } ----
1229 ----
1230 PotentialMatches.clear(); 0
1231 SDWAOperands.clear(); 0
1232 ----
1233 Changed = !ConvertedInstructions.empty(); 0
1234 ----
1235 if (Changed) 0
1236 Ret = true; 0
1237 while (!ConvertedInstructions.empty()) 0
1238 legalizeScalarOperands(*ConvertedInstructions.pop_back_val(), ST); 0
1239 } while (Changed); ----
1240 } ----
1241 ----
1242 return Ret; 0
1243 } ----
1244 ----

521 std::unique_ptr 521 std::unique_ptr
522 SIPeepholeSDWA::matchSDWAOperand(MachineInstr &MI) { 522 SIPeepholeSDWA::matchSDWAOperand(MachineInstr &MI) {
523 unsigned Opcode = MI.getOpcode(); 523 unsigned Opcode = MI.getOpcode();
524 switch (Opcode) { 524 switch (Opcode) {
525 case AMDGPU::V_LSHRREV_B32_e32: 525 case AMDGPU::V_LSHRREV_B32_e32:
526 case AMDGPU::V_ASHRREV_I32_e32: 526 case AMDGPU::V_ASHRREV_I32_e32:
527 case AMDGPU::V_LSHLREV_B32_e32: 527 case AMDGPU::V_LSHLREV_B32_e32:
528 case AMDGPU::V_LSHRREV_B32_e64: 528 case AMDGPU::V_LSHRREV_B32_e64:
529 case AMDGPU::V_ASHRREV_I32_e64: 529 case AMDGPU::V_ASHRREV_I32_e64:
530 case AMDGPU::V_LSHLREV_B32_e64: { 530 case AMDGPU::V_LSHLREV_B32_e64: {
531 // from: v_lshrrev_b32_e32 v1, 16/24, v0 531 // from: v_lshrrev_b32_e32 v1, 16/24, v0
532 // to SDWA src:v0 src_sel:WORD_1/BYTE_3 532 // to SDWA src:v0 src_sel:WORD_1/BYTE_3
533 533
534 // from: v_ashrrev_i32_e32 v1, 16/24, v0 534 // from: v_ashrrev_i32_e32 v1, 16/24, v0
